## `com.daml.ledger.javaapi.data.CommandsSubmission`

- Introduced: `3.4.8`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://javadoc.io/doc/com.daml/bindings-java/3.4.11/com/daml/ledger/javaapi/data/CommandsSubmission.html)

### Signature

```text
public final class CommandsSubmission extends Object
```

### Summary

This class can be used to build a valid submission. It provides create(String, String, Optional, List) for initial creation and methods to set optional parameters e.g withActAs(List), withWorkflowId(String) etc. Usage: var submission = CommandsSubmission.create(userId, commandId, Optional.of(synchronizerId), commands) .withAccessToken(token) .withWorkflowId(workflowId) .with...

- Removed: -

### Signature

```text
public static enum Filter.Interface extends Enum<Filter.Interface>
```

### Summary

Settings for including an interface in CumulativeFilter. There are four possible values: HIDE_VIEW_HIDE_CREATED_EVENT_BLOB and INCLUDE_VIEW_HIDE_CREATED_EVENT_BLOB and HIDE_VIEW_INCLUDE_CREATED_EVENT_BLOB and INCLUDE_VIEW_INCLUDE_CREATED_EVENT_BLOB.

## `com.daml.ledger.javaapi.data.ReassignmentCommands`

- Introduced: `3.4.8`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://javadoc.io/doc/com.daml/bindings-java/3.4.11/com/daml/ledger/javaapi/data/ReassignmentCommands.html)

### Signature

```text
public final class ReassignmentCommands extends Object
```

### Summary

This class can be used to build a valid submission. It provides create(String, String, String, UnassignCommand) for initial creation and methods to set optional parameters e.g withWorkflowId(String), withSubmissionId(String) etc. Usage: var submission = ReassignmentCommands.create(userId, commandId, synchronizerId, unassingnCommand) .withWorkflowId(workflowId) .with...

## `com.daml.ledger.javaapi.data.Transaction.WrappedTransactionTree`

- Introduced: `3.4.8`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://javadoc.io/doc/com.daml/bindings-java/3.4.11/com/daml/ledger/javaapi/data/Transaction.WrappedTransactionTree.html)

### Signature

```text
public static class Transaction.WrappedTransactionTree<WrappedEvent> extends Object
```

### Summary

A generic class that encapsulates a transaction tree along with a list of the wrapped root events of the tree. The wrapped root events are used to construct the tree that is described by the transaction as a tree of WrappedEvents.

## `com.daml.ledger.javaapi.data.UpdateSubmission`

- Introduced: `3.4.8`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://javadoc.io/doc/com.daml/bindings-java/3.4.11/com/daml/ledger/javaapi/data/UpdateSubmission.html)

### Signature

```text
public final class UpdateSubmission<U> extends Object
```

### Summary

This class can be used to build a valid submission for an Update. It provides create(String, String, Update) for initial creation and methods to set optional parameters e.g withActAs(List), withWorkflowId(String) etc. Usage: var submission = UpdateSubmission.create(userId, commandId, update) .withAccessToken(token) .withParty(party) .with...
